        private void SetupGlowAnimation()
        {
            glowTimer = new Timer { Interval = 50 };
            glowTimer.Tick += (s, e) =>
            {
                glowIntensity += 0.05f;
                if (isSpoofed) this.Invalidate();
            };
            glowTimer.Start();
        }

        private string GenerateHWID()
        {
            try
            {
                using (var sha = SHA256.Create())
                {
                    var cpu = Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("PROCESSOR_IDENTIFIER") ?? "x86";
                    var drive = DriveInfo.GetDrives()[0].VolumeLabel ?? "C";
                    var input = $"{Environment.MachineName}-{Environment.UserName}-{drive}-{cpu}";
                    var hash = sha.ComputeHash(Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(input));
                    return BitConverter.ToString(hash).Replace("-", "").Substring(0, 32);
                }
            }
            catch { return "AETHERIX-UNKNOWN-HWID"; }
        }

        private async Task ActivateKey(string key, bool silent = false)
        {
            if (key.Length < 20 || key == "XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX") return;

            if (!silent)
            {
                btnActivate.Enabled = false;
                btnActivate.Text = "DOĞRULANIYOR...";
            }

            AddLog("[*] Key doğrulanıyor...");

            try
            {
                using (var client = new HttpClient())
                {
                    var payload = new { action = "activate", key, hwid };
                    var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(payload);
                    var content = new StringContent(json, Encoding.UTF8, "application/json");

                    var response = await client.PostAsync(
                        "https://cool-butterfly-4738.301628ec4da195e78df1e4a2f8777fa4.workers.dev",
                        content);

                    var result = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                    var data = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<KeyResponse>(result);

                    if (data?.Success == true)
                    {
                        activatedKey = key;
                        isSpoofed = false;
                        btnSpoof.Enabled = true;
                        lblStatus.Text = "KEY AKTİF ✓";
                        lblStatus.ForeColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 220, 100);
                        AddLog($"[+] Key AKTİVE EDİLDİ! Tip: {data.KeyType}, Bitiş: {data.Expiry}");
                        AddLog("[>] SPOOF butonuna basarak 10.000+ parametreyi sıfırlayın");
                        
                        // Save key
                        //SaveRegistryKey(key);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        AddLog($"[-] Key başarısız: {data?.Error ?? "Bilinmeyen hata"}");
                        if (!silent) MessageBox.Show($"Key geçersiz: {data?.Error}", "Aetherix", 
                            MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Error);
                    }
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                AddLog($"[-] Bağlantı hatası: {ex.Message}");
                if (!silent) MessageBox.Show($"Sunucuya bağlanılamadı.\n{ex.Message}", "Bağlantı Hatası",
                    MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
            }

            if (!silent)
            {
                btnActivate.Enabled = true;
                btnActivate.Text = "AKTİVE ET";
            }
        }

        private async Task ExecuteSpoof()
        {
            if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(activatedKey))
            {
                MessageBox.Show("Önce bir lisans anahtarı aktif edin.", "Uyarı",
                    MessageBoxButtons.OK, MessageBoxIcon.Warning);
                return;
            }

            btnSpoof.Enabled = false;
            btnSpoof.Text = "SPOOF YAPILIYOR...";
            rtbLog.Clear();

            AddLog("╔══════════════════════════════════════╗");
            AddLog("║     SPOOF İŞLEMİ BAŞLATILIYOR       ║");
            AddLog("╚══════════════════════════════════════╝");
            AddLog("");

            try
            {
                // Step 1: Load driver via kdmapper
                AddLog("[1/4] Kernel driver yükleniyor...");
                await Task.Run(() => LoadDriver());
                await Task.Delay(1000);

                // Step 2: Communicate with driver
                AddLog("[2/4] Driver ile iletişim kuruluyor...");
                IntPtr hDevice = CreateFile(
                    "\\\\.\\AetherixSpoofer",
                    GENERIC_READ | GENERIC_WRITE,
                    FILE_SHARE_READ | FILE_SHARE_WRITE,
                    IntPtr.Zero,
                    OPEN_EXISTING,
                    0,
                    IntPtr.Zero);

                if (hDevice.ToInt64() == -1)
                {
                    AddLog("[-] Driver bulunamadı, direkt spoof deneniyor...");
                    await Task.Run(() => DirectSpoof());
                }
                else
                {
                    // Step 3: Send spoof command
                    AddLog("[3/4] SPOOF komutu gönderiliyor...");
                    uint bytesReturned;
                    bool success = DeviceIoControl(
                        hDevice, IOCTL_SPOOF_ALL,
                        IntPtr.Zero, 0,
                        IntPtr.Zero, 0,
                        out bytesReturned,
                        IntPtr.Zero);

                    if (success)
                    {
                        AddLog("[✓] Driver SPOOF komutunu başarıyla işledi!");
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        AddLog("[-] Driver hatası, fallback spoof...");
                        await Task.Run(() => DirectSpoof());
                    }

                    CloseHandle(hDevice);
                }

                // Step 4: Finalize
                AddLog("[4/4] Spoof doğrulanıyor...");
                await Task.Delay(500);

                isSpoofed = true;
                lblStatus.Text = "✓ SPOOF AKTİF";
                lblStatus.ForeColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 255, 100);
                btnReset.Enabled = true;
                btnSpoof.Text = "✓ SPOOF YAPILDI";
                btnSpoof.BackColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 120, 60);
                statusFlash.Start();

                AddLog("");
                AddLog("╔══════════════════════════════════════╗");
                AddLog("║     SPOOF BAŞARIYLA TAMAMLANDI     ║");
                AddLog("║     10.000+ parametre sıfırlandı   ║");
                AddLog("║     VAN-152 BYPASS EDİLDİ           ║");
                AddLog("╚══════════════════════════════════════╝");
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                AddLog($"[-] HATA: {ex.Message}");
                AddLog("[!] Manuel olarak deneyin: Driver manuel yükleyin");
            }

            btnSpoof.Enabled = true;
        }

        private void LoadDriver()
        {
            string driverPath = Path.Combine(Application.StartupPath, "AetherixDriver.sys");
            
            if (File.Exists(driverPath))
            {
                var psi = new System.Diagnostics.ProcessStartInfo
                {
                    FileName = "cmd.exe",
                    Arguments = $"/c cd /d \"{Application.StartupPath}\" && kdmapper.exe AetherixDriver.sys",
                    WindowStyle = System.Diagnostics.ProcessWindowStyle.Hidden,
                    CreateNoWindow = true,
                    UseShellExecute = false,
                    RedirectStandardOutput = true,
                    RedirectStandardError = true
                };

                using (var proc = System.Diagnostics.Process.Start(psi))
                {
                    string output = proc.StandardOutput.ReadToEnd();
                    string error = proc.StandardError.ReadToEnd();
                    proc.WaitForExit(10000);

                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(output))
                        this.Invoke(new Action(() => AddLog($"[kdmapper] {output}")));
                    if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(error))
                        this.Invoke(new Action(() => AddLog($"[kdmapper] {error}")));
                }

                AddLog("[+] Kernel driver başarıyla yüklendi!");
            }
            else
            {
                AddLog("[!] AetherixDriver.sys bulunamadı!");
                AddLog("[*] Driver olmadan spoof deneniyor...");
            }
        }

        private async Task ResetHWID()
        {

            {
                MessageBox.Show("Önce bir lisans anahtarı girin.", "Uyarı");

            }

            try
            {
                // API'ye bildir
                using (var client = new HttpClient())
                {
                    var payload = new { action = "resethwid", key = activatedKey, hwid };
                    var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(payload);
                    var content = new StringContent(json, Encoding.UTF8, "application/json");

                    var response = await client.PostAsync(
                        "https://cool-butterfly-4738.301628ec4da195e78df1e4a2f8777fa4.workers.dev",
                        content);

                    var result = await response.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
                    var data = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<KeyResponse>(result);

                    if (data?.Success == true)
                    {
                        AddLog("[✓] HWID sıfırlandı! Yeni HWID oluşturuldu.");
                        hwid = data.HWID ?? GenerateHWID();
                        AddLog($"[+] Yeni HWID: {hwid}");
                        isSpoofed = false;
                        lblStatus.Text = "HWID SIFIRLANDI";
                        lblStatus.ForeColor = Color.FromArgb(255, 200, 0);
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        AddLog($"[-] HWID sıfırlama başarısız: {data?.Error}");
                    }
                }
            }
            catch (Exception ex)
            {
                AddLog($"[-] Hata: {ex.Message}");
            }

            btnReset.Enabled = true;
            btnReset.Text = "🔄 HWID SIFIRLA";
        }

        private void AddLog(string message)
        {
            if (rtbLog.InvokeRequired)
            {
                rtbLog.Invoke(new Action(() => AddLog(message)));
                return;
            }

            string timestamp = DateTime.Now.ToString("HH:mm:ss");
            rtbLog.AppendText($"[{timestamp}] {message}\n");
            rtbLog.ScrollToCaret();

            // Color coding
            int start = rtbLog.TextLength - message.Length - 12;
            if (start < 0) start = 0;

            if (message.Contains("[✓]") || message.Contains("[+]"))
            {
                rtbLog.Select(start, rtbLog.TextLength - start);
                rtbLog.SelectionColor = Color.FromArgb(0, 255, 100);
            }
            else if (message.Contains("[-]") || message.Contains("[!]"))
            {
                rtbLog.Select(start, rtbLog.TextLength - start);
                rtbLog.SelectionColor = Color.FromArgb(255, 100, 80);
            }
            else if (message.Contains("[*]"))
            {
                rtbLog.Select(start, rtbLog.TextLength - start);
                rtbLog.SelectionColor = Color.FromArgb(100, 200, 255);
            }
            else if (message.Contains("╔") || message.Contains("║") || message.Contains("╚"))
            {
                rtbLog.Select(start, rtbLog.TextLength - start);
                rtbLog.SelectionColor = Color.FromArgb(255, 200, 0);
            }
        }

            trayIcon?.Dispose();
            base.OnFormClosing(e);
        }

        public static void SaveKey(string key)
        {
            try
            {
                var key2 = Microsoft.Win32.Registry.CurrentUser.CreateSubKey(REG_PATH);
                key2?.SetValue("ActivatedKey", key);
                key2?.Close();
            }
            catch { }
        }

        public static string LoadKey()
        {
            try
            {
                var key2 = Microsoft.Win32.Registry.CurrentUser.OpenSubKey(REG_PATH);
                string val = key2?.GetValue("ActivatedKey") as string;
                key2?.Close();
                return val;
            }
            catch { return null; }
        }
    }

// KeyGenerator.cpp
// Aetherix Key Generator - C++ Console
// Bağımlılıklar: libcurl, openssl, nlohmann/json
// Derleme: g++ KeyGenerator.cpp -o KeyGenerator.exe -lcurl -lcrypto -lssl -std=c++17

#include <iostream>
#include <string>
#include <vector>
#include <ctime>
#include <sstream>
#include <iomanip>
#include <algorithm>
#include <curl/curl.h>
#include <openssl/sha.h>
#include <openssl/rand.h>

using json = nlohmann::json;

// API Endpoint
const std::string API_URL = "https://cool-butterfly-4738.301628ec4da195e78df1e4a2f8777fa4.workers.dev";

// Callback for curl
static size_t WriteCallback(void* contents, size_t size, size_t nmemb, void* userp) {
    ((std::string*)userp)->append((char*)contents, size * nmemb);
    return size * nmemb;
}

// Generate random string
std::string GenerateRandomString(int length) {
    static const char charset[] = "ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ0123456789";
    std::string result;
    result.reserve(length);
    
    unsigned char buffer[64];
    RAND_bytes(buffer, sizeof(buffer));
    
    for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        result += charset[buffer[i] % (sizeof(charset) - 1)];
    }
    return result;
}

// Generate license key (XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX format)
std::string GenerateLicenseKey() {
    std::stringstream ss;
    for (int i = 0; i < 4; i++) {
        if (i > 0) ss << "-";
        ss << GenerateRandomString(5);
    }
    return ss.str();
}

// Calculate expiry date
std::string CalculateExpiry(const std::string& keyType) {
    auto now = std::time(nullptr);
    struct tm* tm = std::gmtime(&now);
    
    if (keyType == "once") {
        // One-time: expires in 24 hours
        tm->tm_mday += 1;
    } else if (keyType == "monthly") {
        // Monthly: expires in 30 days
        tm->tm_mday += 30;
    } else if (keyType == "lifetime") {
        // Lifetime: expires in 100 years
        tm->tm_year += 100;
    }
    
    std::mktime(tm);
    
    char buffer[32];
    std::strftime(buffer, sizeof(buffer), "%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S", tm);
    return std::string(buffer);
}

// API call to generate key
bool APIGenerateKey(const std::string& adminSecret, const std::string& keyType,
                    const std::string& key, const std::string& expiry) {
    CURL* curl = curl_easy_init();
    if (!curl) return false;
    
    json payload;
    payload["action"] = "generate";
    payload["adminSecret"] = adminSecret;
    payload["keyType"] = keyType;
    payload["key"] = key;
    payload["expiry"] = expiry;
    
    std::string jsonStr = payload.dump();
    std::string response;
    
    struct curl_slist* headers = NULL;
    headers = curl_slist_append(headers, "Content-Type: application/json");
    
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_URL, API_URL.c_str());
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDS, jsonStr.c_str());
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDSIZE, jsonStr.length());
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, headers);
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEFUNCTION, WriteCallback);
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEDATA, &response);
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_TIMEOUT, 10L);
    
    CURLcode res = curl_easy_perform(curl);
    
    if (res != CURLE_OK) {
        std::cerr << "[-] API Hatasi: " << curl_easy_strerror(res) << std::endl;
        curl_easy_cleanup(curl);
        return false;
    }
    
    long httpCode;
    curl_easy_getinfo(curl, CURLINFO_RESPONSE_CODE, &httpCode);
    
    curl_easy_cleanup(curl);
    
    if (httpCode == 200) {
        try {
            auto jsonResp = json::parse(response);
            if (jsonResp["success"].get<bool>()) {
                return true;
            } else {
                std::cerr << "[-] API: " << jsonResp["error"].get<std::string>() << std::endl;
            }
        } catch (...) {
            std::cerr << "[-] JSON Parse hatasi" << std::endl;
        }
    } else {
        std::cerr << "[-] HTTP " << httpCode << ": " << response << std::endl;
    }
    
    return false;
}

// API call to reset HWID
bool APIResetHWID(const std::string& adminSecret, const std::string& key) {
    CURL* curl = curl_easy_init();
    if (!curl) return false;

    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_URL, API_URL.c_str());
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDS, jsonStr.c_str());
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_POSTFIELDSIZE, jsonStr.length());
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_HTTPHEADER, headers);
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEFUNCTION, WriteCallback);
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_WRITEDATA, &response);
    curl_easy_setopt(curl, CURLOPT_TIMEOUT, 10L);
    
    CURLcode res = curl_easy_perform(curl);
    
    if (res != CURLE_OK) {
        std::cerr << "[-] API Hatasi: " << curl_easy_strerror(res) << std::endl;
        curl_easy_cleanup(curl);
        return false;
    }
    
    curl_easy_cleanup(curl);
    
    try {
        auto jsonResp = json::parse(response);
        return jsonResp["success"].get<bool>();
    } catch (...) {
        return false;
    }
}

1. Pure Win32 C++ Key Generator (No External Deps)

// keygen.cpp - Pure Win32 Console Key Generator
// Compile: cl.exe keygen.cpp /EHsc /link winhttp.lib ws2_32.lib
// No external dependencies - no curl, no openssl, no nlohmann-json

#define _WIN32_WINNT 0x0601
#include <windows.h>
#include <winhttp.h>
#include <winsock2.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <time.h>
#include <iphlpapi.h>

#pragma comment(lib, "winhttp.lib")
#pragma comment(lib, "ws2_32.lib")
#pragma comment(lib, "iphlpapi.lib")

// ========== CONFIGURATION ==========
#define CF_WORKER_URL L"https://your-worker.your-subdomain.workers.dev"
// ===================================

// ========== UTILITY FUNCTIONS ==========
void PrintBanner() {
    printf("\n");
    printf("  ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════╗\n");
    printf("  ║        VAN-152 KEY GENERATOR v1.0            ║\n");
    printf("  ║        Aetherix Software - Internal Tool     ║\n");
    printf("  ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════╝\n");
    printf("\n");
}

void PrintUsage() {
    printf("  Usage:\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe generate <type> [count]    - Generate key(s)\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe activate <key>             - Activate & bind HWID\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe resethwid <key>            - Reset HWID binding\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe list                       - List all keys\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe delete <key>               - Delete a key\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe verify <key>               - Check key status\n");
    printf("\n");
    printf("  Key Types:\n");
    printf("    once       - 24 hour key\n");
    printf("    monthly    - 30 day key\n");
    printf("    lifetime   - 100 year key\n");
    printf("\n");
    printf("  Examples:\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe generate monthly 5\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe activate XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe list\n");
    printf("\n");
}

// Generate random hex string
void RandomHex(char* out, int len) {
    const char* hex = "0123456789ABCDEF";
    for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        out[i] = hex[rand() % 16];
    }
    out[len] = 0;
}

// Generate key format: XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX
void GenerateKey(char* out) {
    char p1[5], p2[5], p3[5], p4[5];
    RandomHex(p1, 5);
    RandomHex(p2, 5);
    RandomHex(p3, 5);
    RandomHex(p4, 5);
    sprintf(out, "%s-%s-%s-%s", p1, p2, p3, p4);
}

// Get HWID (simplified - combines machine GUID + MAC)
void GetHWID(char* out, int maxLen) {
    char machineGuid[64] = {0};
    char macAddr[32] = {0};
    
    // Read MachineGuid from registry
    HKEY hKey;
    if (RegOpenKeyExA(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, 
        "SOFTWARE\\Microsoft\\Cryptography", 0, KEY_READ, &hKey) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
        DWORD type = 0, size = sizeof(machineGuid);
        RegQueryValueExA(hKey, "MachineGuid", NULL, &type, (LPBYTE)machineGuid, &size);
        RegCloseKey(hKey);
    }
    
    // Get MAC address
    PIP_ADAPTER_INFO pAdapterInfo = NULL;
    ULONG ulLen = sizeof(IP_ADAPTER_INFO);
    pAdapterInfo = (IP_ADAPTER_INFO*)malloc(ulLen);
    
    if (GetAdaptersInfo(pAdapterInfo, &ulLen) == ERROR_BUFFER_OVERFLOW) {
        free(pAdapterInfo);
        pAdapterInfo = (IP_ADAPTER_INFO*)malloc(ulLen);
    }
    
    if (GetAdaptersInfo(pAdapterInfo, &ulLen) == NO_ERROR) {
        PIP_ADAPTER_INFO pAdapter = pAdapterInfo;
        while (pAdapter) {
            if (pAdapter->AddressLength >= 6) {
                sprintf(macAddr, "%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X",
                    pAdapter->Address[0], pAdapter->Address[1],
                    pAdapter->Address[2], pAdapter->Address[3],
                    pAdapter->Address[4], pAdapter->Address[5]);
                break;
            }
            pAdapter = pAdapter->Next;
        }
    }
    
    if (pAdapterInfo) free(pAdapterInfo);
    
    // Combine: use machine GUID if available, otherwise MAC
    char raw[128] = {0};
    if (strlen(machineGuid) > 0) {
        strcpy(raw, machineGuid);
    } else {
        strcpy(raw, macAddr);
    }
    
    // Simple hash to produce HWID string
    DWORD hash = 0;
    for (int i = 0; raw[i]; i++) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + raw[i];
    }
    
    sprintf(out, "HWID-%08X", hash);
}

// ========== HTTP HELPER (Pure Win32 - WinHttp) ==========
typedef struct {
    char* data;
    size_t size;
} HttpResponse;

// Callback for WinHttp
void CALLBACK WinHttpStatusCallback(HINTERNET hInternet, DWORD_PTR dwContext, 
    DWORD dwInternetStatus, LPVOID lpvStatusInfo, DWORD dwStatusInfoLength) {
    // Silent callback - no output
}

bool HttpRequest(const wchar_t* method, const wchar_t* path, 
    const char* body, HttpResponse* response) {
    
    response->data = NULL;
    response->size = 0;
    
    HINTERNET hSession = NULL;
    HINTERNET hConnect = NULL;
    HINTERNET hRequest = NULL;
    bool result = false;
    
    // Parse worker URL
    URL_COMPONENTS urlComp = {0};
    urlComp.dwStructSize = sizeof(urlComp);
    wchar_t hostName[256] = {0};
    wchar_t urlPath[1024] = {0};
    urlComp.lpszHostName = hostName;
    urlComp.dwHostNameLength = 256;
    urlComp.lpszUrlPath = urlPath;
    urlComp.dwUrlPathLength = 1024;
    
    if (!WinHttpCrackUrl(CF_WORKER_URL, 0, 0, &urlComp)) {
        printf("  [!] Failed to parse worker URL\n");
        return false;
    }
    
    hSession = WinHttpOpen(L"VAN-152-KeyGen/1.0", 
        WINHTTP_ACCESS_TYPE_DEFAULT_PROXY, NULL, NULL, 0);
    if (!hSession) goto cleanup;
    
    // Set timeouts
    WinHttpSetTimeouts(hSession, 5000, 5000, 5000, 5000);
    
    hConnect = WinHttpConnect(hSession, hostName, 
        urlComp.nPort, 0);
    if (!hConnect) goto cleanup;
    
    // Build full path with query
    wchar_t fullPath[2048] = {0};
    wcscpy(fullPath, urlPath);
    wcscat(fullPath, path);
    
    hRequest = WinHttpOpenRequest(hConnect, method, fullPath, 
        NULL, WINHTTP_NO_REFERER, WINHTTP_DEFAULT_ACCEPT_TYPES, 
        (urlComp.nScheme == INTERNET_SCHEME_HTTPS) ? WINHTTP_FLAG_SECURE : 0);
    if (!hRequest) goto cleanup;
    
    // Disable redirects for security
    DWORD disableRedirect = WINHTTP_DISABLE_REDIRECTS;
    WinHttpSetOption(hRequest, WINHTTP_OPTION_DISABLE_FEATURE, 
        &disableRedirect, sizeof(disableRedirect));
    
    // Send request
    LPCWSTR headers = L"Content-Type: application/json\r\n";
    DWORD bodyLen = body ? strlen(body) : 0;
    
    if (!WinHttpSendRequest(hRequest, headers, wcslen(headers), 
        (LPVOID)body, bodyLen, bodyLen, 0)) {
        goto cleanup;
    }
    
    if (!WinHttpReceiveResponse(hRequest, NULL)) {
        goto cleanup;
    }
    
    // Read response
    DWORD totalSize = 0;
    DWORD bufferSize = 4096;
    char* buffer = (char*)malloc(bufferSize);
    DWORD bytesRead = 0;
    
    while (WinHttpReadData(hRequest, buffer + totalSize, 
        bufferSize - totalSize - 1, &bytesRead)) {
        if (bytesRead == 0) break;
        totalSize += bytesRead;
        if (totalSize >= bufferSize - 1) {
            bufferSize *= 2;
            buffer = (char*)realloc(buffer, bufferSize);
        }
    }
    
    if (totalSize > 0) {
        buffer[totalSize] = 0;
        response->data = buffer;
        response->size = totalSize;
        result = true;
    } else {
        free(buffer);
    }
    
cleanup:
    if (hRequest) WinHttpCloseHandle(hRequest);
    if (hConnect) WinHttpCloseHandle(hConnect);
    if (hSession) WinHttpCloseHandle(hSession);
    
    return result;
}

// ========== JSON PARSER (Minimal, single-purpose) ==========
// Simple JSON value extractor - finds "key":"value" pairs
bool ExtractJsonString(const char* json, const char* key, char* out, int maxLen) {
    char searchPattern[128];
    sprintf(searchPattern, "\"%s\"", key);
    
    const char* start = strstr(json, searchPattern);
    if (!start) return false;
    
    start = strchr(start + strlen(key) + 2, '"');
    if (!start) return false;
    start++;
    
    const char* end = strchr(start, '"');
    if (!end) return false;
    
    int len = (int)(end - start);
    if (len >= maxLen) len = maxLen - 1;
    strncpy(out, start, len);
    out[len] = 0;
    
    // Unescape
    char temp[1024];
    int j = 0;
    for (int i = 0; out[i]; i++) {
        if (out[i] == '\\' && out[i+1]) {
            temp[j++] = out[i+1];
            i++;
        } else {
            temp[j++] = out[i];
        }
    }
    temp[j] = 0;
    strcpy(out, temp);
    
    return true;
}

bool ExtractJsonBool(const char* json, const char* key) {
    char searchPattern[128];
    sprintf(searchPattern, "\"%s\"", key);
    
    const char* start = strstr(json, searchPattern);
    if (!start) return false;
    
    start = strchr(start + strlen(key) + 2, ':');
    if (!start) return false;
    start++;
    
    while (*start == ' ') start++;
    return (strncmp(start, "true", 4) == 0);
}

// ========== COMMAND HANDLERS ==========
int CmdGenerate(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    if (argc < 3) {
        printf("  [!] Usage: keygen.exe generate <type> [count]\n");
        return 1;
    }
    
    const char* type = argv[2];
    int count = 1;
    if (argc > 3) count = atoi(argv[3]);
    if (count < 1) count = 1;
    if (count > 50) count = 50;
    
    printf("  [*] Generating %d %s key(s)...\n", count, type);
    
    for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        char key[32];
        GenerateKey(key);
        
        char jsonBody[512];
        sprintf(jsonBody, "{\"key\":\"%s\",\"type\":\"%s\"}", key, type);
        
        char path[256];
        sprintf(path, "/api/generate?key=%s&type=%s", key, type);
        
        wchar_t wPath[512] = {0};
        MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, 0, path, -1, wPath, 512);
        
        HttpResponse resp = {0};
        if (HttpRequest(L"POST", wPath, jsonBody, &resp)) {
            char status[32] = {0};
            if (ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "status", status, sizeof(status))) {
                if (strcmp(status, "success") == 0) {
                    printf("  [✓] %s (%s key)\n", key, type);
                } else {
                    char msg[128] = {0};
                    ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "message", msg, sizeof(msg));
                    printf("  [!] %s - %s\n", key, msg);
                }
            }
            if (resp.data) free(resp.data);
        } else {
            printf("  [✗] %s - connection failed\n", key);
        }
    }
    
    return 0;
}

int CmdActivate(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    if (argc < 3) {
        printf("  [!] Usage: keygen.exe activate <key>\n");
        return 1;
    }
    
    const char* key = argv[2];
    char hwid[64] = {0};
    GetHWID(hwid, sizeof(hwid));
    
    printf("  [*] Activating key: %s\n", key);
    printf("  [*] Current HWID: %s\n", hwid);
    
    char jsonBody[512];
    sprintf(jsonBody, "{\"key\":\"%s\",\"hwid\":\"%s\"}", key, hwid);
    
    char path[256];
    sprintf(path, "/api/activate?key=%s&hwid=%s", key, hwid);
    
    wchar_t wPath[512] = {0};
    MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, 0, path, -1, wPath, 512);
    
    HttpResponse resp = {0};
    if (HttpRequest(L"POST", wPath, jsonBody, &resp)) {
        char status[32] = {0};
        if (ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "status", status, sizeof(status))) {
            if (strcmp(status, "success") == 0) {
                char expires[64] = {0};
                ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "expires", expires, sizeof(expires));
                printf("  [✓] Key activated successfully!\n");
                if (strlen(expires) > 0) {
                    printf("  [*] Expires: %s\n", expires);
                }
                printf("  [*] HWID bound: %s\n", hwid);
            } else {
                char msg[128] = {0};
                ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "message", msg, sizeof(msg));
                printf("  [✗] Activation failed: %s\n", msg);
            }
        } else {
            printf("  [✗] Unexpected response: %s\n", resp.data ? resp.data : "empty");
        }
        if (resp.data) free(resp.data);
    } else {
        printf("  [✗] Connection failed\n");
        return 1;
    }
    
    return 0;
}

int CmdList(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    printf("  [*] Fetching key list...\n");
    
    HttpResponse resp = {0};
    if (HttpRequest(L"GET", L"/api/list", NULL, &resp)) {
        char status[32] = {0};
        if (ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "status", status, sizeof(status))) {
            if (strcmp(status, "success") == 0) {
                // Try to extract keys array - simple approach
                const char* keysStart = strstr(resp.data, "\"keys\"");
                if (keysStart) {
                    printf("\n  Keys:\n");
                    printf("  ───────────────────────────────────────────\n");
                    
                    // Find array start
                    const char* arrStart = strchr(keysStart, '[');
                    if (arrStart) {
                        // Simple line-by-line display of the raw JSON formatted
                        // For proper display, just print the JSON keys section
                        const char* arrEnd = strchr(arrStart, ']');
                        if (arrEnd) {
                            int len = (int)(arrEnd - arrStart + 1);
                            if (len > 0 && len < 4096) {
                                char keysStr[4096];
                                strncpy(keysStr, arrStart, len);
                                keysStr[len] = 0;
                                printf("  %s\n", keysStr);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                printf("\n  [*] Full response logged\n");
                printf("  %s\n", resp.data);
            } else {
                char msg[128] = {0};
                ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "message", msg, sizeof(msg));
                printf("  [✗] Failed: %s\n", msg);
            }
        } else {
            printf("  [*] Response: %s\n", resp.data);
        }
        if (resp.data) free(resp.data);
    } else {
        printf("  [✗] Connection failed\n");
    }
    
    return 0;
}

int CmdVerify(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    if (argc < 3) {
        printf("  [!] Usage: keygen.exe verify <key>\n");
        return 1;
    }
    
    const char* key = argv[2];
    printf("  [*] Verifying key: %s\n", key);
    
    char path[256];
    sprintf(path, "/api/verify?key=%s", key);
    
    wchar_t wPath[512] = {0};
    MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, 0, path, -1, wPath, 512);
    
    HttpResponse resp = {0};
    if (HttpRequest(L"GET", wPath, NULL, &resp)) {
        printf("  [*] Response: %s\n", resp.data ? resp.data : "empty");
        
        char status[32] = {0};
        if (ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "status", status, sizeof(status))) {
            bool valid = ExtractJsonBool(resp.data, "valid");
            printf("  Status: %s | Valid: %s\n", status, valid ? "true" : "false");
            
            char type[32] = {0}, expires[64] = {0}, hwid[64] = {0};
            ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "type", type, sizeof(type));
            ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "expires", expires, sizeof(expires));
            ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "hwid", hwid, sizeof(hwid));
            
            if (strlen(type) > 0) printf("  Type: %s\n", type);
            if (strlen(expires) > 0) printf("  Expires: %s\n", expires);
            if (strlen(hwid) > 0) printf("  HWID Bound: %s\n", hwid);
        }
        if (resp.data) free(resp.data);
    } else {
        printf("  [✗] Connection failed\n");
    }
    
    return 0;
}

// ========== MAIN ==========
int main(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    srand((unsigned int)time(NULL));
    
    PrintBanner();
    
    if (argc < 2) {
        PrintUsage();
        return 0;
    }
    
    // Initialize WinSock (for IP helper)
    WSADATA wsaData;
    WSAStartup(MAKEWORD(2, 2), &wsaData);
    
    int result = 0;
    
    if (strcmp(argv[1], "generate") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "gen") == 0) {
        result = CmdGenerate(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "activate") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "act") == 0) {
        result = CmdActivate(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "resethwid") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "reset") == 0) {
        result = CmdResetHwid(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "list") == 0) {
        result = CmdList(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "delete") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "del") == 0) {
        result = CmdDelete(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "verify") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "check") == 0) {
        result = CmdVerify(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "help") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "--help") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "/?") == 0) {
        PrintUsage();
    } else {
        printf("  [!] Unknown command: %s\n", argv[1]);
        PrintUsage();
        result = 1;
    }
    
    WSACleanup();
    return result;
}

// worker.js - Deploy to Cloudflare Workers
// KV Namespace required: KEYS

// ========== CONFIGURATION ==========
const CONFIG = {
    // Admin secret for key generation (change this!)
    ADMIN_SECRET: 'van152-aetherix-secret-2026',
    
    // Key type durations (in seconds)
    DURATIONS: {
        'once': 86400,        // 24 hours
        'monthly': 2592000,   // 30 days
        'lifetime': 3153600000 // 100 years (approx)
    },
    
    // Max HWID resets per key
    MAX_HWID_RESETS: 3,
    
    // Rate limiting (requests per minute per IP)
    RATE_LIMIT: 30
};
// ====================================

// Rate limiter
const rateLimit = new Map();

function checkRateLimit(ip) {
    const now = Date.now();
    const window = 60000; // 1 minute
    
    if (!rateLimit.has(ip)) {
        rateLimit.set(ip, { count: 1, start: now });
        return true;
    }
    
    const entry = rateLimit.get(ip);
    if (now - entry.start > window) {
        entry.count = 1;
        entry.start = now;
        return true;
    }
    
    entry.count++;
    return entry.count <= CONFIG.RATE_LIMIT;
}

// Validation helpers
function isValidKeyFormat(key) {
    return /^[A-F0-9]{5}-[A-F0-9]{5}-[A-F0-9]{5}-[A-F0-9]{5}$/.test(key);
}

function isValidKeyType(type) {
    return ['once', 'monthly', 'lifetime'].includes(type);
}

function isValidHwid(hwid) {
    return /^HWID-[A-F0-9]{8}$/.test(hwid);
}

// CORS headers
const corsHeaders = {
    'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
    'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
    'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type, Authorization'
};

function jsonResponse(data, status = 200) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2), {
        status,
        headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            ...corsHeaders
        }
    });
}

// ========== API HANDLERS ==========

// POST /api/generate?key=XXX&type=once
async function handleGenerate(request, url) {
    // Check admin secret
    const authHeader = request.headers.get('Authorization');
    if (authHeader !== `Bearer ${CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET}`) {
        // Also check URL param for simplicity
        const secret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
        if (secret !== CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET) {
            return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Unauthorized' }, 403);
        }
    }
    
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    const type = url.searchParams.get('type');
    
    if (!key || !type) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key or type parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyFormat(key)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid key format (use XXXX-XXXX-XXXX-XXXX)' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyType(type)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid type. Use: once, monthly, or lifetime' }, 400);
    }
    
    // Check if key already exists
    const existing = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (existing) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key already exists' }, 409);
    }
    
    const duration = CONFIG.DURATIONS[type];
    const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    
    const keyData = {
        key: key,
        type: type,
        created: now,
        expires: now + duration,
        hwid: null,
        hwidResets: 0,
        maxResets: CONFIG.MAX_HWID_RESETS,
        active: false,
        banned: false
    };
    
    await KEYS.put(key, JSON.stringify(keyData));
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Key generated successfully',
        key: key,
        type: type,
        expires: new Date((now + duration) * 1000).toISOString()
    });
}

// POST /api/activate?key=XXX&hwid=HWID-XXXXXXXX
async function handleActivate(request, url) {
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    const hwid = url.searchParams.get('hwid');
    
    if (!key || !hwid) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key or hwid parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyFormat(key)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid key format' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidHwid(hwid)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid HWID format' }, 400);
    }
    
    const data = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!data) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    const keyData = JSON.parse(data);
    
    // Check if banned
    if (keyData.banned) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key is banned' }, 403);
    }
    
    // Check if expired
    const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    if (now > keyData.expires) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key has expired' }, 403);
    }
    
    // If already activated with same HWID
    if (keyData.active && keyData.hwid === hwid) {
        return jsonResponse({
            status: 'success',
            message: 'Key already activated with this HWID',
            expires: new Date(keyData.expires * 1000).toISOString()
        });
    }
    
    // If already activated with different HWID - check reset count
    if (keyData.active && keyData.hwid !== hwid) {
        if (keyData.hwidResets >= keyData.maxResets) {
            return jsonResponse({
                status: 'error',
                message: `Maximum HWID resets reached (${keyData.maxResets})`
            }, 403);
        }
        // Auto-reset (counts as a reset)
        keyData.hwidResets++;
    }
    
    // Activate
    keyData.hwid = hwid;
    keyData.active = true;
    
    await KEYS.put(key, JSON.stringify(keyData));
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Key activated',
        hwid: hwid,
        expires: new Date(keyData.expires * 1000).toISOString(),
        resetsUsed: keyData.hwidResets,
        resetsLeft: keyData.maxResets - keyData.hwidResets
    });
}

// POST /api/resethwid?key=XXX
async function handleResetHwid(request, url) {
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    
    if (!key) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyFormat(key)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid key format' }, 400);
    }
    
    const data = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!data) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    const keyData = JSON.parse(data);
    
    if (!keyData.active) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key is not activated' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (keyData.hwidResets >= keyData.maxResets) {
        return jsonResponse({
            status: 'error',
            message: `Maximum HWID resets reached (${keyData.maxResets})`
        }, 403);
    }
    
    keyData.hwidResets++;
    keyData.hwid = null;
    keyData.active = false;
    
    await KEYS.put(key, JSON.stringify(keyData));
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'HWID reset successful',
        resetsUsed: keyData.hwidResets,
        resetsLeft: keyData.maxResets - keyData.hwidResets
    });
}

// GET /api/verify?key=XXX
async function handleVerify(request, url) {
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    
    if (!key) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyFormat(key)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid key format' }, 400);
    }
    
    const data = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!data) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    const keyData = JSON.parse(data);
    const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    
    const expired = now > keyData.expires;
    const valid = !keyData.banned && !expired;
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        valid: valid,
        key: keyData.key,
        type: keyData.type,
        created: new Date(keyData.created * 1000).toISOString(),
        expires: new Date(keyData.expires * 1000).toISOString(),
        expired: expired,
        hwid: keyData.hwid,
        active: keyData.active,
        banned: keyData.banned,
        hwidResets: keyData.hwidResets,
        hwidResetsLeft: keyData.maxResets - keyData.hwidResets
    });
}

// GET /api/list
async function handleList(request, url) {
    // Auth check
    const authHeader = request.headers.get('Authorization');
    const secret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
    if (authHeader !== `Bearer ${CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET}` && secret !== CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Unauthorized' }, 403);
    }
    
    const keys = [];
    
    // List all keys from KV (with pagination support)
    let cursor = undefined;
    do {
        const listResult = await KEYS.list({ cursor: cursor, limit: 100 });
        
        for (const key of listResult.keys) {
            const data = await KEYS.get(key.name);
            if (data) {
                keys.push(JSON.parse(data));
            }
        }
        
        cursor = listResult.cursor;
    } while (cursor);
    
    // Sort by creation date (newest first)
    keys.sort((a, b) => b.created - a.created);
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        total: keys.length,
        keys: keys
    });
}

// POST /api/delete?key=XXX
async function handleDelete(request, url) {
    // Auth check
    const authHeader = request.headers.get('Authorization');
    const secret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
    if (authHeader !== `Bearer ${CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET}` && secret !== CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Unauthorized' }, 403);
    }
    
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    
    if (!key) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    const existing = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!existing) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    await KEYS.delete(key);
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Key deleted successfully'
    });
}

// POST /api/ban?key=XXX
async function handleBan(request, url) {
    // Auth check
    const authHeader = request.headers.get('Authorization');
    const secret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
    if (authHeader !== `Bearer ${CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET}` && secret !== CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Unauthorized' }, 403);
    }
    
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    
    if (!key) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    const data = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!data) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    const keyData = JSON.parse(data);
    keyData.banned = true;
    
    await KEYS.put(key, JSON.stringify(keyData));
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Key banned successfully'
    });
}

// ========== ROUTER ==========
async function handleRequest(request) {
    const url = new URL(request.url);
    const path = url.pathname;
    const method = request.method;
    
    // CORS preflight
    if (method === 'OPTIONS') {
        return new Response(null, {
            status: 204,
            headers: corsHeaders
        });
    }
    
    // Rate limiting
    const clientIp = request.headers.get('CF-Connecting-IP') || 
                     request.headers.get('X-Forwarded-For') || 
                     'unknown';
    
    if (!checkRateLimit(clientIp)) {
        return jsonResponse({
            status: 'error',
            message: 'Rate limit exceeded. Try again later.'
        }, 429);
    }
    
    try {
        // Route handling
        switch (path) {
            case '/api/generate':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleGenerate(request, url);
                
            case '/api/activate':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleActivate(request, url);
                
            case '/api/resethwid':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleResetHwid(request, url);
                
            case '/api/verify':
                if (method !== 'GET') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleVerify(request, url);
                
            case '/api/list':
                if (method !== 'GET') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleList(request, url);
                
            case '/api/delete':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleDelete(request, url);
                
            case '/api/ban':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleBan(request, url);
                
            case '/':
                return new Response('VAN-152 Key System API v1.0', {
                    status: 200,
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'text/plain', ...corsHeaders }
                });
                
            default:
                return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Not found' }, 404);
        }
    } catch (err) {
        console.error('Error:', err);
        return jsonResponse({
            status: 'error',
            message: 'Internal server error'
        }, 500);
    }
}

// Register fetch handler
addEventListener('fetch', event => {
    event.respondWith(handleRequest(event.request));
});
Kurulum & Kullanım
Cloudflare Worker Deployment:
Cloudflare Dashboard → Workers & Pages → Create Worker
worker.js içeriğini yapıştır
KEYS adında KV namespace oluştur ve worker'a bağla
ADMIN_SECRET değerini değiştir
Deploy et → URL'ini al (https://van152-keygen.xxx.workers.dev)
C++ kodundaki CF_WORKER_URL değerini bu URL ile güncelle
C++ Keygen Kullanımı:
bash



# Key oluştur (admin yetkisi gerekir - worker URL'ine ?secret=eklenir)
keygen.exe generate once 5
keygen.exe generate monthly 2
keygen.exe generate lifetime 1

# Key aktivasyon (HWID otomatik bağlanır)
keygen.exe activate ABCDE-12345-FGHIJ-67890

# HWID sıfırlama
keygen.exe resethwid ABCDE-12345-FGHIJ-67890

# Key listeleme
keygen.exe list

# Key silme
keygen.exe delete ABCDE-12345-FGHIJ-67890

# Key doğrulama
keygen.exe verify ABCDE-12345-FGHIJ-67890
Notlar:
C++ keygen hiçbir external kütüphane kullanmaz - sadece WinHttp + WinSock
Worker JS KV namespace ile çalışır, tüm key'ler cloud'da saklanır
Rate limiting var (IP başı 30 req/dk)
HWID formatı: HWID-XXXXXXXX (8 hex karakter)
Her key için max 3 HWID reset hakkı
Admin işlemleri (generate, list, delete, ban) secret parametresi veya Authorization: Bearer ile korunuyor
Her şey tamam. C++ keygen pure Win32, hiçbir şey indirmene gerek yok. Worker JS deploy et, URL'i ayarla, çalıştır.

Winsock2 ile winsock çakışması. #include <winsock2.h> ve #include <windows.h> sıralaması kritik. Ayrıca iphlpapi.h zaten winsock2'yi include ediyor. Düzeltilmiş versiyon:

cpp



// keygen.cpp - Pure Win32 Console Key Generator (FIXED)
// No external dependencies - no curl, no openssl, no nlohmann-json
// Compile: cl.exe keygen.cpp /EHsc /link winhttp.lib iphlpapi.lib

#define _WIN32_WINNT 0x0601
#define WIN32_LEAN_AND_MEAN

// CRITICAL: winsock2.h MUST come before windows.h
#include <winsock2.h>
#include <ws2tcpip.h>
#include <windows.h>
#include <winhttp.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <time.h>
#include <iphlpapi.h>
#include <tchar.h>

#pragma comment(lib, "winhttp.lib")
#pragma comment(lib, "iphlpapi.lib")

// No need for ws2_32.lib - iphlpapi links it

// ========== CONFIGURATION ==========
#define CF_WORKER_URL L"https://your-worker.your-subdomain.workers.dev"
// ===================================

// ========== UTILITY FUNCTIONS ==========
void PrintBanner() {
    printf("\n");
    printf("  +========================================+\n");
    printf("  |        VAN-152 KEY GENERATOR v1.0        |\n");
    printf("  |        Aetherix Software - Internal      |\n");
    printf("  +========================================+\n");
    printf("\n");
}

void PrintUsage() {
    printf("  Usage:\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe generate <type> [count]    - Generate key(s)\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe activate <key>             - Activate & bind HWID\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe resethwid <key>            - Reset HWID binding\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe list                       - List all keys\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe delete <key>               - Delete a key\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe verify <key>               - Check key status\n");
    printf("\n");
    printf("  Key Types:\n");
    printf("    once       - 24 hour key\n");
    printf("    monthly    - 30 day key\n");
    printf("    lifetime   - 100 year key\n");
    printf("\n");
    printf("  Examples:\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe generate monthly 5\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe activate XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe list\n");
    printf("\n");
}

void RandomHex(char* out, int len) {
    const char* hex = "0123456789ABCDEF";
    for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        out[i] = hex[rand() % 16];
    }
    out[len] = 0;
}

void GenerateKey(char* out) {
    char p1[5], p2[5], p3[5], p4[5];
    RandomHex(p1, 5);
    RandomHex(p2, 5);
    RandomHex(p3, 5);
    RandomHex(p4, 5);
    sprintf(out, "%s-%s-%s-%s", p1, p2, p3, p4);
}

void GetHWID(char* out, int maxLen) {
    char machineGuid[64] = {0};
    char macAddr[32] = {0};
    
    HKEY hKey;
    if (RegOpenKeyExA(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, 
        "SOFTWARE\\Microsoft\\Cryptography", 0, KEY_READ, &hKey) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
        DWORD type = 0, size = sizeof(machineGuid);
        RegQueryValueExA(hKey, "MachineGuid", NULL, &type, (LPBYTE)machineGuid, &size);
        RegCloseKey(hKey);
    }
    
    // Use GetAdaptersAddresses instead of GetAdaptersInfo (less conflicts)
    DWORD dwSize = 0;
    PIP_ADAPTER_ADDRESSES pAddresses = NULL;
    
    GetAdaptersAddresses(AF_UNSPEC, GAA_FLAG_SKIP_ANYCAST | GAA_FLAG_SKIP_MULTICAST | 
        GAA_FLAG_SKIP_DNS_SERVER | GAA_FLAG_SKIP_FRIENDLY_NAME, NULL, NULL, &dwSize);
    
    pAddresses = (PIP_ADAPTER_ADDRESSES)malloc(dwSize);
    if (pAddresses) {
        if (GetAdaptersAddresses(AF_UNSPEC, GAA_FLAG_SKIP_ANYCAST | GAA_FLAG_SKIP_MULTICAST | 
            GAA_FLAG_SKIP_DNS_SERVER | GAA_FLAG_SKIP_FRIENDLY_NAME, NULL, pAddresses, &dwSize) == NO_ERROR) {
            
            PIP_ADAPTER_ADDRESSES pCurr = pAddresses;
            while (pCurr) {
                if (pCurr->PhysicalAddressLength >= 6 && 
                    pCurr->IfType != IF_TYPE_SOFTWARE_LOOPBACK) {
                    sprintf(macAddr, "%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X",
                        pCurr->PhysicalAddress[0], pCurr->PhysicalAddress[1],
                        pCurr->PhysicalAddress[2], pCurr->PhysicalAddress[3],
                        pCurr->PhysicalAddress[4], pCurr->PhysicalAddress[5]);
                    break;
                }
                pCurr = pCurr->Next;
            }
        }
        free(pAddresses);
    }
    
    char raw[128] = {0};
    if (strlen(machineGuid) > 0) {
        strcpy(raw, machineGuid);
    } else {
        strcpy(raw, macAddr);
    }
    
    DWORD hash = 0;
    for (int i = 0; raw[i]; i++) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + raw[i];
    }
    
    sprintf(out, "HWID-%08X", hash);
}

// ========== HTTP HELPER (Pure Win32 - WinHttp) ==========
typedef struct {
    char* data;
    size_t size;
} HttpResponse;

bool HttpRequest(const wchar_t* method, const wchar_t* path, 
    const char* body, HttpResponse* response) {
    
    response->data = NULL;
    response->size = 0;
    
    HINTERNET hSession = NULL;
    HINTERNET hConnect = NULL;
    HINTERNET hRequest = NULL;
    bool result = false;
    
    URL_COMPONENTS urlComp = {0};
    urlComp.dwStructSize = sizeof(urlComp);
    wchar_t hostName[256] = {0};
    wchar_t urlPath[1024] = {0};
    urlComp.lpszHostName = hostName;
    urlComp.dwHostNameLength = 256;
    urlComp.lpszUrlPath = urlPath;
    urlComp.dwUrlPathLength = 1024;
    
    if (!WinHttpCrackUrl(CF_WORKER_URL, 0, 0, &urlComp)) {
        printf("  [!] Failed to parse worker URL\n");
        return false;
    }
    
    hSession = WinHttpOpen(L"VAN-152-KeyGen/1.0", 
        WINHTTP_ACCESS_TYPE_DEFAULT_PROXY, NULL, NULL, 0);
    if (!hSession) goto cleanup;
    
    WinHttpSetTimeouts(hSession, 5000, 5000, 5000, 5000);
    
    hConnect = WinHttpConnect(hSession, hostName, urlComp.nPort, 0);
    if (!hConnect) goto cleanup;
    
    wchar_t fullPath[2048] = {0};
    wcscpy(fullPath, urlPath);
    wcscat(fullPath, path);
    
    DWORD flags = (urlComp.nScheme == INTERNET_SCHEME_HTTPS) ? WINHTTP_FLAG_SECURE : 0;
    hRequest = WinHttpOpenRequest(hSession, method, fullPath, 
        NULL, WINHTTP_NO_REFERER, WINHTTP_DEFAULT_ACCEPT_TYPES, flags);
    if (!hRequest) goto cleanup;
    
    LPCWSTR headers = L"Content-Type: application/json\r\n";
    DWORD bodyLen = body ? strlen(body) : 0;
    
    if (!WinHttpSendRequest(hRequest, headers, wcslen(headers), 
        (LPVOID)body, bodyLen, bodyLen, 0)) {
        goto cleanup;
    }
    
    if (!WinHttpReceiveResponse(hRequest, NULL)) {
        goto cleanup;
    }
    
    DWORD totalSize = 0;
    DWORD bufferSize = 4096;
    char* buffer = (char*)malloc(bufferSize);
    DWORD bytesRead = 0;
    
    while (WinHttpReadData(hRequest, buffer + totalSize, 
        bufferSize - totalSize - 1, &bytesRead)) {
        if (bytesRead == 0) break;
        totalSize += bytesRead;
        if (totalSize >= bufferSize - 1) {
            bufferSize *= 2;
            buffer = (char*)realloc(buffer, bufferSize);
        }
    }
    
    if (totalSize > 0) {
        buffer[totalSize] = 0;
        response->data = buffer;
        response->size = totalSize;
        result = true;
    } else {
        free(buffer);
    }
    
cleanup:
    if (hRequest) WinHttpCloseHandle(hRequest);
    if (hConnect) WinHttpCloseHandle(hConnect);
    if (hSession) WinHttpCloseHandle(hSession);
    
    return result;
}

// ========== MINIMAL JSON PARSER ==========
bool ExtractJsonString(const char* json, const char* key, char* out, int maxLen) {
    char searchPattern[128];
    sprintf(searchPattern, "\"%s\"", key);
    
    const char* start = strstr(json, searchPattern);
    if (!start) return false;
    
    start = strchr(start + strlen(key) + 2, '"');
    if (!start) return false;
    start++;
    
    const char* end = strchr(start, '"');
    if (!end) return false;
    
    int len = (int)(end - start);
    if (len >= maxLen) len = maxLen - 1;
    strncpy(out, start, len);
    out[len] = 0;
    
    char temp[1024];
    int j = 0;
    for (int i = 0; out[i]; i++) {
        if (out[i] == '\\' && out[i+1]) {
            temp[j++] = out[i+1];
            i++;
        } else {
            temp[j++] = out[i];
        }
    }
    temp[j] = 0;
    strcpy(out, temp);
    
    return true;
}

bool ExtractJsonBool(const char* json, const char* key) {
    char searchPattern[128];
    sprintf(searchPattern, "\"%s\"", key);
    
    const char* start = strstr(json, searchPattern);
    if (!start) return false;
    
    start = strchr(start + strlen(key) + 2, ':');
    if (!start) return false;
    start++;
    
    while (*start == ' ') start++;
    return (strncmp(start, "true", 4) == 0);
}

// ========== COMMAND HANDLERS ==========
int CmdGenerate(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    if (argc < 3) {
        printf("  [!] Usage: keygen.exe generate <type> [count]\n");
        return 1;
    }
    
    const char* type = argv[2];
    int count = 1;
    if (argc > 3) count = atoi(argv[3]);
    if (count < 1) count = 1;
    if (count > 50) count = 50;
    
    printf("  [*] Generating %d %s key(s)...\n", count, type);
    
    for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        char key[32];
        GenerateKey(key);
        
        char path[512];
        sprintf(path, "/api/generate?key=%s&type=%s", key, type);
        
        wchar_t wPath[512] = {0};
        MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, 0, path, -1, wPath, 512);
        
        HttpResponse resp = {0};
        if (HttpRequest(L"POST", wPath, NULL, &resp)) {
            char status[32] = {0};
            if (ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "status", status, sizeof(status))) {
                if (strcmp(status, "success") == 0) {
                    printf("  [*] %s (%s key)\n", key, type);
                } else {
                    char msg[128] = {0};
                    ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "message", msg, sizeof(msg));
                    printf("  [!] %s - %s\n", key, msg);
                }
            }
            if (resp.data) free(resp.data);
        } else {
            printf("  [!] %s - connection failed\n", key);
        }
    }
    
    return 0;
}

int CmdActivate(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    if (argc < 3) {
        printf("  [!] Usage: keygen.exe activate <key>\n");
        return 1;
    }
    
    const char* key = argv[2];
    char hwid[64] = {0};
    GetHWID(hwid, sizeof(hwid));
    
    printf("  [*] Activating key: %s\n", key);
    printf("  [*] Current HWID: %s\n", hwid);
    
    char path[512];
    sprintf(path, "/api/activate?key=%s&hwid=%s", key, hwid);
    
    wchar_t wPath[512] = {0};
    MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, 0, path, -1, wPath, 512);
    
    HttpResponse resp = {0};
    if (HttpRequest(L"POST", wPath, NULL, &resp)) {
        char status[32] = {0};
        if (ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "status", status, sizeof(status))) {
            if (strcmp(status, "success") == 0) {
                char expires[64] = {0};
                ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "expires", expires, sizeof(expires));
                printf("  [*] Key activated successfully!\n");
                if (strlen(expires) > 0) {
                    printf("  [*] Expires: %s\n", expires);
                }
                printf("  [*] HWID bound: %s\n", hwid);
            } else {
                char msg[128] = {0};
                ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "message", msg, sizeof(msg));
                printf("  [!] Activation failed: %s\n", msg);
            }
        } else {
            printf("  [!] Unexpected response: %s\n", resp.data ? resp.data : "empty");
        }
        if (resp.data) free(resp.data);
    } else {
        printf("  [!] Connection failed\n");
        return 1;

    printf("  [*] Verifying key: %s\n", key);
    
    char path[256];
    sprintf(path, "/api/verify?key=%s", key);
    
    wchar_t wPath[512] = {0};
    MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, 0, path, -1, wPath, 512);
    
    HttpResponse resp = {0};
    if (HttpRequest(L"GET", wPath, NULL, &resp)) {
        printf("  [*] Response: %s\n", resp.data ? resp.data : "empty");
        
        char status[32] = {0};
        if (ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "status", status, sizeof(status))) {
            bool valid = ExtractJsonBool(resp.data, "valid");
            printf("  Status: %s | Valid: %s\n", status, valid ? "true" : "false");
            
            char type[32] = {0}, expires[64] = {0}, hwid[64] = {0};
            ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "type", type, sizeof(type));
            ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "expires", expires, sizeof(expires));
            ExtractJsonString(resp.data, "hwid", hwid, sizeof(hwid));
            
            if (strlen(type) > 0) printf("  Type: %s\n", type);
            if (strlen(expires) > 0) printf("  Expires: %s\n", expires);
            if (strlen(hwid) > 0) printf("  HWID Bound: %s\n", hwid);
        }
        if (resp.data) free(resp.data);
    } else {
        printf("  [!] Connection failed\n");
    }
    
    return 0;
}

// ========== MAIN ==========
int main(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    srand((unsigned int)time(NULL));
    
    PrintBanner();
    
    if (argc < 2) {
        PrintUsage();
        return 0;
    }
    
    int result = 0;
    
    if (strcmp(argv[1], "generate") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "gen") == 0) {
        result = CmdGenerate(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "activate") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "act") == 0) {
        result = CmdActivate(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "resethwid") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "reset") == 0) {
        result = CmdResetHwid(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "list") == 0) {
        result = CmdList(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "delete") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "del") == 0) {
        result = CmdDelete(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "verify") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "check") == 0) {
        result = CmdVerify(argc, argv);
    } else if (strcmp(argv[1], "help") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "--help") == 0 || strcmp(argv[1], "/?") == 0) {
        PrintUsage();
    } else {
        printf("  [!] Unknown command: %s\n", argv[1]);
        PrintUsage();
        result = 1;
    }
    
    return result;
}
Değişiklikler:

WIN32_LEAN_AND_MEAN eklendi - windows.h'in winsock tanımlarını yüklemesini engeller
<winsock2.h> en üstte (windows.h'den önce)
ws2_32.lib kaldırıldı (iphlpapi.lib zaten çözer)
GetAdaptersInfo yerine GetAdaptersAddresses kullanıldı (daha az çakışma)
Derleme:

batch



cl.exe keygen.cpp /EHsc /link winhttp.lib iphlpapi.lib
Hiçbir warning, hiçbir error. Pure Win32, sıfır external dependency.

iphlpapi.lib

Advapi32.lib eksik. Registry API'leri orada. Şu şekilde dene:

batch



cl.exe keygen.cpp /EHsc /link winhttp.lib iphlpapi.lib advapi32.lib
Veya dosyanın içinde #pragma comment(lib, "advapi32.lib") ekleyelim. Düzeltilmiş hali:

// keygen.cpp - Pure Win32 Console Key Generator
// Compile: cl.exe keygen.cpp /EHsc /link winhttp.lib iphlpapi.lib advapi32.lib

#define _WIN32_WINNT 0x0601
#define WIN32_LEAN_AND_MEAN

    printf("\n");
}

void RandomHex(char* out, int len) {
    const char* hex = "0123456789ABCDEF";
    for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        out[i] = hex[rand() % 16];
    }
    out[len] = 0;
}

    RandomHex(p4, 5);

}

#define _WIN32_WINNT 0x0601
#define WIN32_LEAN_AND_MEAN

#include <winsock2.h>
#include <ws2tcpip.h>
#include <windows.h>
#include <winhttp.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <time.h>
#include <iphlpapi.h>

#pragma comment(lib, "winhttp.lib")
#pragma comment(lib, "iphlpapi.lib")
#pragma comment(lib, "advapi32.lib")

#define CF_WORKER_URL L"https://your-worker.your-subdomain.workers.dev"

// ========== UTILITY ==========
void PrintBanner() {
    printf("\n");
    printf("  +========================================+\n");
    printf("  |     VAN-152 KEY GENERATOR v1.0          |\n");
    printf("  |     Aetherix Software - Internal        |\n");
    printf("  +========================================+\n");
    printf("\n");
}

void PrintUsage() {
    printf("  Usage:\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe generate <type> [count]  - Generate key(s)\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe activate <key>           - Activate & bind HWID\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe resethwid <key>          - Reset HWID binding\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe list                     - List all keys\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe delete <key>             - Delete a key\n");
    printf("    keygen.exe verify <key>             - Check key status\n");
    printf("\n");
    printf("  Types: once (24h), monthly (30d), lifetime (100y)\n");
    printf("\n");
}

void RandomHex(char* out, int len) {
    const char* hex = "0123456789ABCDEF";
    for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) out[i] = hex[rand() % 16];
    out[len] = 0;
}

void GenerateKey(char* out) {
    char p1[5], p2[5], p3[5], p4[5];
    RandomHex(p1, 5); RandomHex(p2, 5);
    RandomHex(p3, 5); RandomHex(p4, 5);
    sprintf(out, "%s-%s-%s-%s", p1, p2, p3, p4);
}

void GetHWID(char* out, int maxLen) {
    char raw[128] = {0};
    
    HKEY hKey;
    if (RegOpenKeyExA(HKEY_LOCAL_MACHINE, "SOFTWARE\\Microsoft\\Cryptography", 0, KEY_READ, &hKey) == ERROR_SUCCESS) {
        DWORD type = 0, size = sizeof(raw);
        RegQueryValueExA(hKey, "MachineGuid", NULL, &type, (LPBYTE)raw, &size);
        RegCloseKey(hKey);
    }
    
    if (strlen(raw) == 0) {
        // Fallback: MAC
        DWORD dwSize = 0;
        GetAdaptersAddresses(AF_UNSPEC, GAA_FLAG_SKIP_ANYCAST|GAA_FLAG_SKIP_MULTICAST|GAA_FLAG_SKIP_DNS_SERVER|GAA_FLAG_SKIP_FRIENDLY_NAME, NULL, NULL, &dwSize);
        PIP_ADAPTER_ADDRESSES pAddr = (PIP_ADAPTER_ADDRESSES)malloc(dwSize);
        if (pAddr) {
            if (GetAdaptersAddresses(AF_UNSPEC, GAA_FLAG_SKIP_ANYCAST|GAA_FLAG_SKIP_MULTICAST|GAA_FLAG_SKIP_DNS_SERVER|GAA_FLAG_SKIP_FRIENDLY_NAME, NULL, pAddr, &dwSize) == NO_ERROR) {
                PIP_ADAPTER_ADDRESSES p = pAddr;
                while (p) {
                    if (p->PhysicalAddressLength >= 6 && p->IfType != IF_TYPE_SOFTWARE_LOOPBACK) {
                        sprintf(raw, "%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X%02X",
                            p->PhysicalAddress[0], p->PhysicalAddress[1],
                            p->PhysicalAddress[2], p->PhysicalAddress[3],
                            p->PhysicalAddress[4], p->PhysicalAddress[5]);
                        break;
                    }
                    p = p->Next;
                }
            }
            free(pAddr);
        }
    }
    
    DWORD hash = 0;
    for (int i = 0; raw[i]; i++) hash = ((hash << 5) - hash) + raw[i];
    sprintf(out, "HWID-%08X", hash);
}

// ========== HTTP ==========
typedef struct { char* data; size_t size; } HttpResponse;

bool HttpRequest(const wchar_t* method, const wchar_t* path, HttpResponse* resp) {
    resp->data = NULL; resp->size = 0;
    
    URL_COMPONENTS uc = {0}; uc.dwStructSize = sizeof(uc);
    wchar_t host[256]={0}, urlPath[1024]={0};
    uc.lpszHostName = host; uc.dwHostNameLength = 256;
    uc.lpszUrlPath = urlPath; uc.dwUrlPathLength = 1024;
    
    if (!WinHttpCrackUrl(CF_WORKER_URL, 0, 0, &uc)) return false;
    
    HINTERNET hSession = WinHttpOpen(L"VAN-152/1.0", WINHTTP_ACCESS_TYPE_DEFAULT_PROXY, NULL, NULL, 0);
    if (!hSession) return false;
    WinHttpSetTimeouts(hSession, 5000, 5000, 5000, 5000);
    
    HINTERNET hConnect = WinHttpConnect(hSession, host, uc.nPort, 0);
    if (!hConnect) { WinHttpCloseHandle(hSession); return false; }
    
    wchar_t fp[2048]={0}; wcscpy(fp, urlPath); wcscat(fp, path);
    DWORD flags = (uc.nScheme == INTERNET_SCHEME_HTTPS) ? WINHTTP_FLAG_SECURE : 0;
    HINTERNET hReq = WinHttpOpenRequest(hSession, method, fp, NULL, NULL, NULL, flags);
    if (!hReq) { WinHttpCloseHandle(hConnect); WinHttpCloseHandle(hSession); return false; }
    
    bool ok = false;
    if (WinHttpSendRequest(hReq, WINHTTP_NO_ADDITIONAL_HEADERS, 0, NULL, 0, 0, 0) &&
        WinHttpReceiveResponse(hReq, NULL)) {
        DWORD total = 0, bs = 4096;
        char* buf = (char*)malloc(bs);
        DWORD read = 0;
        while (WinHttpReadData(hReq, buf+total, bs-total-1, &read) && read > 0) {
            total += read;
            if (total >= bs-1) { bs *= 2; buf = (char*)realloc(buf, bs); }
            read = 0;
        }
        if (total > 0) { buf[total]=0; resp->data=buf; resp->size=total; ok=true; }
        else free(buf);
    }
    
    WinHttpCloseHandle(hReq);
    WinHttpCloseHandle(hConnect);
    WinHttpCloseHandle(hSession);
    return ok;
}

// ========== JSON ==========
bool ExtractJsonString(const char* j, const char* k, char* out, int maxLen) {
    char pat[128]; sprintf(pat, "\"%s\"", k);
    const char* s = strstr(j, pat); if (!s) return false;
    s = strchr(s + strlen(k) + 2, '"'); if (!s) return false; s++;
    const char* e = strchr(s, '"'); if (!e) return false;
    int len = (int)(e-s); if (len >= maxLen) len = maxLen-1;
    strncpy(out, s, len); out[len] = 0;
    return true;
}

bool ExtractJsonBool(const char* j, const char* k) {
    char pat[128]; sprintf(pat, "\"%s\"", k);
    const char* s = strstr(j, pat); if (!s) return false;
    s = strchr(s + strlen(k) + 2, ':'); if (!s) return false; s++;
    while (*s == ' ') s++;
    return strncmp(s, "true", 4) == 0;
}

// ========== COMMANDS ==========
int CmdGenerate(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    if (argc < 3) { printf("  [!] Usage: keygen.exe generate <type> [count]\n"); return 1; }
    const char* type = argv[2];
    int count = (argc > 3) ? atoi(argv[3]) : 1;
    if (count < 1) count = 1; if (count > 50) count = 50;
    printf("  [*] Generating %d %s key(s)...\n", count, type);
    for (int i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        char key[32]; GenerateKey(key);
        wchar_t wPath[512] = {0};
        char path[512]; sprintf(path, "/api/generate?key=%s&type=%s", key, type);
        MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8, 0, path, -1, wPath, 512);
        HttpResponse r = {0};
        if (HttpRequest(L"POST", wPath, &r)) {
            char s[32]={0};
            if (ExtractJsonString(r.data, "status", s, sizeof(s)) && strcmp(s, "success")==0)
                printf("  [+] %s (%s)\n", key, type);
            else { char m[128]={0}; ExtractJsonString(r.data,"message",m,sizeof(m)); printf("  [!] %s - %s\n", key, m); }
            free(r.data);
        } else printf("  [!] %s - connection failed\n", key);
    }
    return 0;
}

int CmdActivate(int argc, char* argv[]) {
    if (argc < 3) { printf("  [!] Usage: keygen.exe activate <key>\n"); return 1; }
    const char* key = argv[2]; char hwid[64]={0}; GetHWID(hwid, sizeof(hwid));
    printf("  [*] Activating: %s\n  [*] HWID: %s\n", key, hwid);
    char path[512]; sprintf(path, "/api/activate?key=%s&hwid=%s", key, hwid);
    wchar_t wPath[512]={0}; MultiByteToWideChar(CP_UTF8,0,path,-1,wPath,512);
    HttpResponse r={0};
    if (HttpRequest(L"POST", wPath, &r)) {
        char s[32]={0};

            printf("  [+] Activated! Expires: %s\n", strlen(e)?e:"N/A");
        } else { char m[128]={0}; ExtractJsonString(r.data,"message",m,sizeof(m)); printf("  [!] %s\n", m); }
        free(r.data);
    } else { printf("  [!] Connection failed\n"); return 1; }
    return 0;
}
