1 kerelik (once)	24 saat geçerli
Aylık (monthly)	30 gün geçerli
Lifetime	100 yıl geçerli (pratikte sonsuz)
Hepsi aynı keygen ile üretiliyor — tek fark keygen.exe <type> komutunda <type> kısmı:

bash



keygen.exe once       # 24 saatlik key üretir
keygen.exe monthly    # 30 günlük key üretir
keygen.exe lifetime   # 100 yıllık key üretir
Her biri XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX-XXXXX formatında hex uppercase key basar. Cloudflare Worker'a kaydederken de type parametresini once, monthly veya lifetime olarak gönderir, Worker da ona göre expiration hesaplar.

Şimdi, son derleme hatası aldın mı keygen'de? advapi32.lib ekleyince düzeldi mi? Hala hata alıyorsan hatanın tam çıktısını at, düzelteyim.

C:\temp\vanguard_bypass\WinFormsApp1\x64\Release>keygen.exe generate lifetime 1

  +========================================+
  |     VAN-152 KEY GENERATOR v1.0          |
  |     Aetherix Software - Internal        |
  +========================================+

  [*] Generating 1 lifetime key(s)...
  [!] D9B79-FFA3B-BED78-8D25D - connection failed reis bu cool-butterfly-4738.301628ec4da195e78df1e4a2f8777fa4.workers.dev KEYS e bağlanamıyo sanki
Bağlantı hatası alıyorsun. Birkaç sebebi olabilir:

Worker URL'i yanlış — cool-butterfly-4738.301628ec4da195e78df1e4a2f8777fa4.workers.dev bu adres doğru mu? Cloudflare Worker'ın deploy ettiğin gerçek URL bu mu?
Worker deploy edilmemiş olabilir — Worker'ı Cloudflare Dashboard'a yükleyip deploy ettin mi?
DNS çözümleme sorunu — DNS henüz yayılmamış olabilir.
Önce şunu dene — browser'da şu URL'i aç:




https://cool-butterfly-4738.301628ec4da195e78df1e4a2f8777fa4.workers.dev/api/health
Geliyor mu? Eğer "Worker not found" veya "404" alıyorsan, Worker ya deploy edilmemiş ya da URL yanlış.

Worker URL'ini doğrulamak için Cloudflare Dashboard'a gir → Workers & Pages → worker'ına tıkla → Preview veya Deploy sekmesinde gösterilen URL'i kullan.

Doğru URL'i aldıktan sonra keygen.cpp'deki CF_WORKER_URL sabitini güncellemen gerek:

cpp



// şu satırı bul:
#define CF_WORKER_URL "cool-butterfly-4738.301628ec4da195e78df1e4a2f8777fa4.workers.dev"

// örnek doğru kullanım:
#define CF_WORKER_URL "van152-key-system.workers.dev"  // gerçek worker adını koy
Worker'ı deploy ettiysen URL ne gösteriyor? Ona göre düzeltelim.

belki js dendir
Haklı olabilirsin. JS'de hata olabilir. Worker kodunu bana atar mısın? Bir bakayım, düzeltirim.

// worker.js - Deploy to Cloudflare Workers
// KV Namespace required: KEYS

// ========== CONFIGURATION ==========
const CONFIG = {
    // Admin secret for key generation (change this!)
    ADMIN_SECRET: 'van152-aetherix-secret-2026',
    
    // Key type durations (in seconds)
    DURATIONS: {
        'once': 86400,        // 24 hours
        'monthly': 2592000,   // 30 days
        'lifetime': 3153600000 // 100 years (approx)
    },
    
    // Max HWID resets per key
    MAX_HWID_RESETS: 3,
    
    // Rate limiting (requests per minute per IP)
    RATE_LIMIT: 30
};
// ====================================

// Rate limiter
const rateLimit = new Map();

function checkRateLimit(ip) {
    const now = Date.now();
    const window = 60000; // 1 minute
    
    if (!rateLimit.has(ip)) {
        rateLimit.set(ip, { count: 1, start: now });
        return true;
    }
    
    const entry = rateLimit.get(ip);
    if (now - entry.start > window) {
        entry.count = 1;
        entry.start = now;
        return true;
    }
    
    entry.count++;
    return entry.count <= CONFIG.RATE_LIMIT;
}

// Validation helpers
function isValidKeyFormat(key) {
    return /^[A-F0-9]{5}-[A-F0-9]{5}-[A-F0-9]{5}-[A-F0-9]{5}$/.test(key);
}

function isValidKeyType(type) {
    return ['once', 'monthly', 'lifetime'].includes(type);
}

function isValidHwid(hwid) {
    return /^HWID-[A-F0-9]{8}$/.test(hwid);
}

// CORS headers
const corsHeaders = {
    'Access-Control-Allow-Origin': '*',
    'Access-Control-Allow-Methods': 'GET, POST, OPTIONS',
    'Access-Control-Allow-Headers': 'Content-Type, Authorization'
};

function jsonResponse(data, status = 200) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify(data, null, 2), {
        status,
        headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
            ...corsHeaders
        }
    });
}

// ========== API HANDLERS ==========

// POST /api/generate?key=XXX&type=once
async function handleGenerate(request, url) {
    // Check admin secret
    const authHeader = request.headers.get('Authorization');
    if (authHeader !== `Bearer ${CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET}`) {
        // Also check URL param for simplicity
        const secret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
        if (secret !== CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET) {
            return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Unauthorized' }, 403);
        }
    }
    
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    const type = url.searchParams.get('type');
    
    if (!key || !type) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key or type parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyFormat(key)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid key format (use XXXX-XXXX-XXXX-XXXX)' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyType(type)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid type. Use: once, monthly, or lifetime' }, 400);
    }
    
    // Check if key already exists
    const existing = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (existing) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key already exists' }, 409);
    }
    
    const duration = CONFIG.DURATIONS[type];
    const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    
    const keyData = {
        key: key,
        type: type,
        created: now,
        expires: now + duration,
        hwid: null,
        hwidResets: 0,
        maxResets: CONFIG.MAX_HWID_RESETS,
        active: false,
        banned: false
    };
    
    await KEYS.put(key, JSON.stringify(keyData));
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Key generated successfully',
        key: key,
        type: type,
        expires: new Date((now + duration) * 1000).toISOString()
    });
}

// POST /api/activate?key=XXX&hwid=HWID-XXXXXXXX
async function handleActivate(request, url) {
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    const hwid = url.searchParams.get('hwid');
    
    if (!key || !hwid) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key or hwid parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyFormat(key)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid key format' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidHwid(hwid)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid HWID format' }, 400);
    }
    
    const data = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!data) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    const keyData = JSON.parse(data);
    
    // Check if banned
    if (keyData.banned) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key is banned' }, 403);
    }
    
    // Check if expired
    const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    if (now > keyData.expires) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key has expired' }, 403);
    }
    
    // If already activated with same HWID
    if (keyData.active && keyData.hwid === hwid) {
        return jsonResponse({
            status: 'success',
            message: 'Key already activated with this HWID',
            expires: new Date(keyData.expires * 1000).toISOString()
        });
    }
    
    // If already activated with different HWID - check reset count
    if (keyData.active && keyData.hwid !== hwid) {
        if (keyData.hwidResets >= keyData.maxResets) {
            return jsonResponse({
                status: 'error',
                message: `Maximum HWID resets reached (${keyData.maxResets})`
            }, 403);
        }
        // Auto-reset (counts as a reset)
        keyData.hwidResets++;
    }
    
    // Activate
    keyData.hwid = hwid;
    keyData.active = true;
    
    await KEYS.put(key, JSON.stringify(keyData));
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Key activated',
        hwid: hwid,
        expires: new Date(keyData.expires * 1000).toISOString(),
        resetsUsed: keyData.hwidResets,
        resetsLeft: keyData.maxResets - keyData.hwidResets
    });
}

// POST /api/resethwid?key=XXX
async function handleResetHwid(request, url) {
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    
    if (!key) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyFormat(key)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid key format' }, 400);
    }
    
    const data = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!data) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    const keyData = JSON.parse(data);
    
    if (!keyData.active) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key is not activated' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (keyData.hwidResets >= keyData.maxResets) {
        return jsonResponse({
            status: 'error',
            message: `Maximum HWID resets reached (${keyData.maxResets})`
        }, 403);
    }
    
    keyData.hwidResets++;
    keyData.hwid = null;
    keyData.active = false;
    
    await KEYS.put(key, JSON.stringify(keyData));
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'HWID reset successful',
        resetsUsed: keyData.hwidResets,
        resetsLeft: keyData.maxResets - keyData.hwidResets
    });
}

// GET /api/verify?key=XXX
async function handleVerify(request, url) {
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    
    if (!key) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    if (!isValidKeyFormat(key)) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Invalid key format' }, 400);
    }
    
    const data = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!data) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    const keyData = JSON.parse(data);
    const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    
    const expired = now > keyData.expires;
    const valid = !keyData.banned && !expired;
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        valid: valid,
        key: keyData.key,
        type: keyData.type,
        created: new Date(keyData.created * 1000).toISOString(),
        expires: new Date(keyData.expires * 1000).toISOString(),
        expired: expired,
        hwid: keyData.hwid,
        active: keyData.active,
        banned: keyData.banned,
        hwidResets: keyData.hwidResets,
        hwidResetsLeft: keyData.maxResets - keyData.hwidResets
    });
}

// GET /api/list
async function handleList(request, url) {
    // Auth check
    const authHeader = request.headers.get('Authorization');
    const secret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
    if (authHeader !== `Bearer ${CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET}` && secret !== CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Unauthorized' }, 403);
    }
    
    const keys = [];
    
    // List all keys from KV (with pagination support)
    let cursor = undefined;
    do {
        const listResult = await KEYS.list({ cursor: cursor, limit: 100 });
        
        for (const key of listResult.keys) {
            const data = await KEYS.get(key.name);
            if (data) {
                keys.push(JSON.parse(data));
            }
        }
        
        cursor = listResult.cursor;
    } while (cursor);
    
    // Sort by creation date (newest first)
    keys.sort((a, b) => b.created - a.created);
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        total: keys.length,
        keys: keys
    });
}

// POST /api/delete?key=XXX
async function handleDelete(request, url) {
    // Auth check
    const authHeader = request.headers.get('Authorization');
    const secret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
    if (authHeader !== `Bearer ${CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET}` && secret !== CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Unauthorized' }, 403);
    }
    
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    
    if (!key) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    const existing = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!existing) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    await KEYS.delete(key);
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Key deleted successfully'
    });
}

// POST /api/ban?key=XXX
async function handleBan(request, url) {
    // Auth check
    const authHeader = request.headers.get('Authorization');
    const secret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
    if (authHeader !== `Bearer ${CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET}` && secret !== CONFIG.ADMIN_SECRET) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Unauthorized' }, 403);
    }
    
    const key = url.searchParams.get('key');
    
    if (!key) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Missing key parameter' }, 400);
    }
    
    const data = await KEYS.get(key);
    if (!data) {
        return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Key not found' }, 404);
    }
    
    const keyData = JSON.parse(data);
    keyData.banned = true;
    
    await KEYS.put(key, JSON.stringify(keyData));
    
    return jsonResponse({
        status: 'success',
        message: 'Key banned successfully'
    });
}

// ========== ROUTER ==========
async function handleRequest(request) {
    const url = new URL(request.url);
    const path = url.pathname;
    const method = request.method;
    
    // CORS preflight
    if (method === 'OPTIONS') {
        return new Response(null, {
            status: 204,
            headers: corsHeaders
        });
    }
    
    // Rate limiting
    const clientIp = request.headers.get('CF-Connecting-IP') || 
                     request.headers.get('X-Forwarded-For') || 
                     'unknown';
    
    if (!checkRateLimit(clientIp)) {
        return jsonResponse({
            status: 'error',
            message: 'Rate limit exceeded. Try again later.'
        }, 429);
    }
    
    try {
        // Route handling
        switch (path) {
            case '/api/generate':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleGenerate(request, url);
                
            case '/api/activate':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleActivate(request, url);
                
            case '/api/resethwid':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleResetHwid(request, url);
                
            case '/api/verify':
                if (method !== 'GET') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleVerify(request, url);
                
            case '/api/list':
                if (method !== 'GET') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleList(request, url);
                
            case '/api/delete':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleDelete(request, url);
                
            case '/api/ban':
                if (method !== 'POST') {
                    return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Method not allowed' }, 405);
                }
                return await handleBan(request, url);
                
            case '/':
                return new Response('VAN-152 Key System API v1.0', {
                    status: 200,
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'text/plain', ...corsHeaders }
                });
                
            default:
                return jsonResponse({ status: 'error', message: 'Not found' }, 404);
        }
    } catch (err) {
        console.error('Error:', err);
        return jsonResponse({
            status: 'error',
            message: 'Internal server error'
        }, 500);
    }
}

// Register fetch handler
addEventListener('fetch', event => {
    event.respondWith(handleRequest(event.request));
});
JS'de sorun var. Şu eksiklikleri gördüm:

/api/health endpoint'i yok — keygen önce health check yapıyor olabilir
Rate limiter memory'de Map kullanıyor, Edge'de her request farklı isolated context'te çalışabilir — rate limit sıfırdan başlar (sorun değil aslında)
Keygen'deki bağlantı kodu POST değil WinHttpOpenRequest ile farklı method kullanıyor olabilir
Asıl sorun şu olabilir — KV Namespace binding'i eksik. Worker'a KV bağlamayı unuttun mu? Worker deploy edildi mi? Şu URL'i browser'da aç:




https://cool-butterfly-4738.301628ec4da195e78df1e4a2f8777fa4.workers.dev/

/* VAN-152 Vanguard Emulator Server
 * Debian 12 - TCP Server - Port 8484 - pthreads
 * Key auth with HWID binding
 * Commands: ACTIVATE, VERIFY, GENERATE, RESET_HWID, BAN, DELETE, HEALTH
 */

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <unistd.h>
#include <arpa/inet.h>
#include <pthread.h>
#include <time.h>
#include <sys/stat.h>
#include <ctype.h>
#include <errno.h>
#include <signal.h>

#define PORT 8484
#define MAX_CLIENTS 256
#define BUFFER_SIZE 4096
#define KEY_STR_LEN 24
#define HWID_STR_LEN 16
#define MAX_KEY_TYPES 3
#define MAX_RESETS 3
#define KEY_FILE "/root/vanguard-emu/server/keys/keys.json"
#define ADMIN_SECRET "van152-aetherix-secret-2026"

typedef enum { KEY_ONCE, KEY_MONTHLY, KEY_LIFETIME } KeyType;

typedef struct {
    char key[KEY_STR_LEN + 1];
    char key_type[16];
    char hwid[HWID_STR_LEN + 1];
    char created[32];
    char expires[32];
    int active;
    int resets_used;
} KeyEntry;

typedef struct {
    KeyEntry *keys;
    int count;
    int capacity;
    pthread_mutex_t mutex;
} KeyDB;

static KeyDB db;
static int server_fd;
static int server_running = 1;

/* --- JSON Parser (minimal, no deps) --- */
static char* json_get_str(const char *json, const char *key) {
    char search[128];
    snprintf(search, sizeof(search), "\"%s\"", key);
    const char *p = strstr(json, search);
    if (!p) return NULL;
    p = strchr(p, ':');
    if (!p) return NULL;
    p++;
    while (*p && isspace(*p)) p++;
    if (*p == '"') {
        p++;
        const char *end = strchr(p, '"');
        if (!end) return NULL;
        size_t len = end - p;
        char *val = malloc(len + 1);
        if (!val) return NULL;
        strncpy(val, p, len);
        val[len] = '\0';
        return val;
    }
    return NULL;
}

static int json_get_int(const char *json, const char *key) {
    char search[128];
    snprintf(search, sizeof(search), "\"%s\"", key);
    const char *p = strstr(json, search);
    if (!p) return 0;
    p = strchr(p, ':');
    if (!p) return 0;
    p++;
    while (*p && isspace(*p)) p++;
    return atoi(p);
}

static char* json_escape(const char *s) {
    size_t len = strlen(s);
    size_t cap = len * 2 + 1;
    char *out = malloc(cap);
    if (!out) return NULL;
    size_t j = 0;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < len; i++) {
        if (s[i] == '"' || s[i] == '\\') out[j++] = '\\';
        out[j++] = s[i];
        if (j >= cap - 2) { cap *= 2; out = realloc(out, cap); }
    }
    out[j] = '\0';
    return out;
}

/* --- Key Generation --- */
static void generate_key_str(char *out) {
    static const char hex[] = "0123456789ABCDEF";
    for (int g = 0; g < 4; g++) {
        if (g > 0) out[g * 6 - 1] = '-';
        for (int i = 0; i < 5; i++)
            out[g * 6 + g + i] = hex[rand() % 16];
    }
    out[23] = '\0';
    /* Verify uniqueness */
    for (int i = 0; i < db.count; i++)
        if (strcmp(out, db.keys[i].key) ==
devam etsene
Tamam, devam ediyorum. server.c'nin kalanı:

            if (strcmp(out, db.keys[i].key) == 0) {
                generate_key_str(out);
                return;
            }
        }
}

static void compute_expiry(const char *type, char *expires, size_t exp_sz) {
    time_t now = time(NULL);
    struct tm *tm = gmtime(&now);
    if (strcmp(type, "once") == 0) now += 86400;
    else if (strcmp(type, "monthly") == 0) now += 86400 * 30;
    else if (strcmp(type, "lifetime") == 0) now += 86400 * 365 * 100;
    tm = gmtime(&now);
    strftime(expires, exp_sz, "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", tm);
}

/* --- Key DB Persistence --- */
static void db_save(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen(KEY_FILE, "w");
    if (!f) { perror("fopen save"); return; }
    fprintf(f, "{\"keys\":[");
    for (int i = 0; i < db.count; i++) {
        if (i > 0) fprintf(f, ",");
        char *e_key = json_escape(db.keys[i].key);
        char *e_type = json_escape(db.keys[i].key_type);
        char *e_hwid = json_escape(db.keys[i].hwid);
        char *e_created = json_escape(db.keys[i].created);
        char *e_expires = json_escape(db.keys[i].expires);
        fprintf(f, "{\"key\":\"%s\",\"type\":\"%s\",\"hwid\":\"%s\","
                   "\"created\":\"%s\",\"expires\":\"%s\","
                   "\"active\":%d,\"resets\":%d}",
                e_key ? e_key : "", e_type ? e_type : "",
                e_hwid ? e_hwid : "", e_created ? e_created : "",
                e_expires ? e_expires : "",
                db.keys[i].active, db.keys[i].resets_used);
        free(e_key); free(e_type); free(e_hwid);
        free(e_created); free(e_expires);
    }
    fprintf(f, "]}");
    fclose(f);
}

static void db_load(void) {
    FILE *f = fopen(KEY_FILE, "r");
    if (!f) {
        db.keys = malloc(sizeof(KeyEntry) * 100);
        db.count = 0;
        db.capacity = 100;
        db_save();
        return;
    }
    fseek(f, 0, SEEK_END);
    long fsize = ftell(f);
    fseek(f, 0, SEEK_SET);
    char *json = malloc(fsize + 1);
    fread(json, 1, fsize, f);
    json[fsize] = '\0';
    fclose(f);
    db.keys = malloc(sizeof(KeyEntry) * 100);
    db.count = 0;
    db.capacity = 100;
    const char *p = json;
    int in_array = 0;
    while (*p) {
        if (*p == '[') in_array = 1;
        else if (*p == '{' && in_array) {
            if (db.count >= db.capacity) {
                db.capacity *= 2;
                db.keys = realloc(db.keys, sizeof(KeyEntry) * db.capacity);
            }
            KeyEntry *e = &db.keys[db.count];
            memset(e, 0, sizeof(KeyEntry));
            char *v = json_get_str(p, "key");
            if (v) { strncpy(e->key, v, KEY_STR_LEN); free(v); }
            v = json_get_str(p, "type");
            if (v) { strncpy(e->key_type, v, 15); free(v); }
            v = json_get_str(p, "hwid");
            if (v) { strncpy(e->hwid, v, HWID_STR_LEN); free(v); }
            v = json_get_str(p, "created");
            if (v) { strncpy(e->created, v, 31); free(v); }
            v = json_get_str(p, "expires");
            if (v) { strncpy(e->expires, v, 31); free(v); }
            e->active = json_get_int(p, "active");
            e->resets_used = json_get_int(p, "resets");
            db.count++;
        }
        p++;
    }
    free(json);
}

/* --- Key Operations --- */
static KeyEntry* find_key(const char *key) {
    for (int i = 0; i < db.count; i++)
        if (strcmp(db.keys[i].key, key) == 0)
            return &db.keys[i];
    return NULL;
}

static int is_expired(KeyEntry *e) {
    struct tm tm;
    time_t exp_time, now;
    memset(&tm, 0, sizeof(tm));
    if (sscanf(e->expires, "%d-%d-%dT%d:%d:%d",
               &tm.tm_year, &tm.tm_mon, &tm.tm_mday,
               &tm.tm_hour, &tm.tm_min, &tm.tm_sec) != 6)
        return 0;
    tm.tm_year -= 1900; tm.tm_mon -= 1;
    exp_time = timegm(&tm);
    now = time(NULL);
    return now > exp_time;
}

/* --- Command Handlers --- */
static char* handle_generate(const char *key_str, const char *type, const char *secret) {
    if (!secret || strcmp(secret, ADMIN_SECRET) != 0)
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Invalid secret\"}");
    if (!type || (strcmp(type, "once") != 0 && strcmp(type, "monthly") != 0 && strcmp(type, "lifetime") != 0))
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Invalid type (once/monthly/lifetime)\"}");
    if (find_key(key_str))
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Key already exists\"}");

    pthread_mutex_lock(&db.mutex);
    if (db.count >= db.capacity) {
        db.capacity *= 2;
        db.keys = realloc(db.keys, sizeof(KeyEntry) * db.capacity);
    }
    KeyEntry *e = &db.keys[db.count];
    memset(e, 0, sizeof(KeyEntry));
    strncpy(e->key, key_str, KEY_STR_LEN);
    strncpy(e->key_type, type, 15);
    time_t now = time(NULL);
    struct tm *tm = gmtime(&now);
    strftime(e->created, sizeof(e->created), "%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ", tm);
    compute_expiry(type, e->expires, sizeof(e->expires));
    e->active = 0;
    e->resets_used = 0;
    db.count++;
    db_save();
    pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);

    char resp[512];
    snprintf(resp, sizeof(resp),
        "{\"status\":\"success\",\"message\":\"Key created\",\"key\":\"%s\",\"type\":\"%s\",\"expires\":\"%s\"}",
        key_str, type, e->expires);
    return strdup(resp);
}

static char* handle_activate(const char *key_str, const char *hwid) {
    if (!key_str || !hwid)
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Missing key or hwid\"}");

    pthread_mutex_lock(&db.mutex);
    KeyEntry *e = find_key(key_str);
    if (!e) {
        pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Key not found\"}");
    }
    if (e->active) {
        if (strcmp(e->hwid, hwid) == 0) {
            pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
            return strdup("{\"status\":\"success\",\"message\":\"Already activated on this HWID\"}");
        }
        pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Key already bound to another HWID\"}");
    }
    if (is_expired(e)) {
        pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Key has expired\"}");
    }

    strncpy(e->hwid, hwid, HWID_STR_LEN);
    e->active = 1;
    db_save();
    pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);

    char resp[512];
    snprintf(resp, sizeof(resp),
        "{\"status\":\"success\",\"message\":\"Key activated\",\"hwid\":\"%s\",\"type\":\"%s\",\"expires\":\"%s\"}",
        hwid, e->key_type, e->expires);
    return strdup(resp);
}

static char* handle_verify(const char *key_str) {
    pthread_mutex_lock(&db.mutex);
    KeyEntry *e = find_key(key_str);
    if (!e) {
        pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Key not found\"}");
    }
    int expired = is_expired(e);
    char resp[512];
    snprintf(resp, sizeof(resp),
        "{\"status\":\"success\",\"key\":\"%s\",\"type\":\"%s\",\"active\":%d,\"hwid\":\"%s\","
        "\"created\":\"%s\",\"expires\":\"%s\",\"expired\":%d,\"resets_used\":%d}",
        e->key, e->key_type, e->active, e->hwid,
        e->created, e->expires, expired, e->resets_used);
    pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
    return strdup(resp);
}

static char* handle_reset_hwid(const char *key_str) {
    pthread_mutex_lock(&db.mutex);
    KeyEntry *e = find_key(key_str);
    if (!e) {
        pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Key not found\"}");
    }
    if (e->resets_used >= MAX_RESETS) {
        pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Max HWID resets reached\"}");
    }
    e->resets_used++;
    e->active = 0;
    memset(e->hwid, 0, HWID_STR_LEN + 1);
    db_save();
    pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
    char resp[256];
    snprintf(resp, sizeof(resp),
        "{\"status\":\"success\",\"message\":\"HWID reset\",\"resets_used\":%d,\"max_resets\":%d}",
        e->resets_used, MAX_RESETS);
    return strdup(resp);
}

static char* handle_ban(const char *key_str, const char *secret) {
    if (!secret || strcmp(secret, ADMIN_SECRET) != 0)
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Invalid secret\"}");
    pthread_mutex_lock(&db.mutex);
    KeyEntry *e = find_key(key_str);
    if (!e) {
        pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Key not found\"}");
    }
    /* Mark as expired permanently */
    strncpy(e->expires, "1970-01-01T00:00:00Z", 31);
    db_save();
    pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
    return strdup("{\"status\":\"success\",\"message\":\"Key banned\"}");
}

static char* handle_delete(const char *key_str, const char *secret) {
    if (!secret || strcmp(secret, ADMIN_SECRET) != 0)
        return strdup("{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Invalid secret\"}");
    pthread_mutex_lock(&db.mutex);
    int found = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i < db.count; i++) {
        if (strcmp(db.keys[i].key, key_str) == 0) {
            memmove(&db.keys[i], &db.keys[i+1], (db.count - i - 1) * sizeof(KeyEntry));
            db.count--;
            found = 1;
            break;
        }
    }
    if (found) db_save();
    pthread_mutex_unlock(&db.mutex);
    return strdup(found ?
        "{\"status\":\"success\",\"message\":\"Key deleted\"}" :
        "{\"status\":\"error\",\"message\":\"Key not found\"}");
}

    /* Count active */
    int idx = 0;
    for (int i = 0; i
